 haalanki petrol-dijal kii keemton ko nirdhaarit karne ke formule ko dekhen to saaf he ki in taxon se sarkaar kii badi aamadani ho rahi he

 Ramdev wants to sell petrol for 35 rupees, permission sought from the government, petrol and diesel are not imported in India
 aayaat mahaj kachche tel kaa kiya jaataa he

 yadi sarkaar ne kachche tel, jo ki petrol-dijal taiyaar karne main kaccha maal he, kii jagah sidhe petrol-dijal kaa aayaat kiya hota, to us rate par port dauty lagaate hue kendra or rajya sarkaron keexiseor waite ko jodakar desh main petrol-dijal ko bechney kaa rate tay kiya jaataa he
 This formula for determining the rate of petrol and diesel is called import parity price
 gauratlab he ki isse pehle 2002 tak desh main petrol-dijal kii keemat nirdhaarit karne ke liye cost-plus formule kaa istemaal kiya jaataa tha
 Under this formula, the central government used to determine the retail rate of petrol and diesel while spending on the purchase of crude oil over a long period
 haalanki is formule kii sabase badi aalochana yah thi ki petrol-dijal kii keemat nirdhaarit karne ke kaam main paardarshita kii kami thi
 At the same time, transparency in the import parity price is high
 lihaaja, 2002 main petrol-dijal kii keemat ko diregulate karte hue bazaar ke hawaale kar diya gaya
 The new formula was then reviewed by the c Rangarajan Committee in 2006 and cited the import parity price as the right way
 emport parity price main yadi kachche tel kii keemat main lagaataar ijapha ho rahaa he to jaahir he petrol-dijal kii keemton main adhik ijapha ho rahaa hoga
 This is because the increase in raw material leads to a greater increase in the price of the product
 sarkaar petrol-dijal par adhik tex vasuul paati he or tel companiyaan ro material main ijaphe ke baad utpaada kii keemat main ijapha karti hai
